        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We are truly delighted to be a part of 𝐍𝐞𝐰𝐥𝐚𝐧𝐝 Team.

Our sincere thanks entire 𝐍𝐞𝐰𝐥𝐚𝐧𝐝 team, and to 𝐍𝐞𝐰𝐥𝐚𝐧𝐝 Türkiye—dear <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/yavuz-sahin-78ba8a15?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Yavuz Sahin</a>, <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/oguzgucarslan?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Oguz GUCARSLAN</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/caglaripek?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Çağlar İpek</a>—for their unwavering support in every situation.
